# Extracted Graph Full Inventory (2026-03-28)

This file inventories the extracted BNY graph from `import/recordeval_graph_extracted.json` and annotates it with the current IDs visible in `http://localhost:3000/api/collection/bootstrap`.

Interpretation rules:

- `current_id` is the currently visible identifier in the rebuilt collection.
- When `current_id` starts with `seed:`, the extracted node is still seed-only in the current collection snapshot.
- `missing_from_app` means the extracted label was not present under the same label in the current collection snapshot.
- `merged_by_er` notes extracted labels that currently collapse to the same ID.
- Relationship rows are sourced from the extracted graph. Their properties are the extracted `timestamp` and `citations` fields.
